\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{Mtc\_ImDbGetImSessionStart()}{Mtc\_ImDbGetImSessionStart()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily Z\+F\+U\+NC Z\+U\+I\+NT Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Db\+Get\+Im\+Session\+Start (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{Z\+F\+U\+N\+C\+\_\+\+V\+O\+ID}]{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}



Get IM parameter when the receiver client/device implementation should return the 200 OK initiating the M\+S\+RP session associated to a 1-\/to-\/1 chat. It is required to be instantiated if a service provider enables 1-\/to-\/1 Chat. 


\begin{DoxyRetVals}{Return values}
{\em 0} & (R\+CS 5.\+1 default)\+: The 200 OK is sent when the receiver consumes the notification by opening the chat window. \\
\hline
{\em 1} & (R\+CS Release 2-\/4 default)\+: The 200 OK is sent when the receiver starts to type a message to be sent back in the chat window. \\
\hline
{\em 2} & (new option)\+: The 200 OK is sent when the receiver presses the button to send a message (That is the message will be buffered in the client until the M\+S\+RP session is established).\\
\hline
\end{DoxyRetVals}
\begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\mbox{\hyperlink{mtc__im__db_8h_aecc6843da565ecbf5c28416915dcd456}{Mtc\+\_\+\+Im\+Db\+Set\+Im\+Session\+Start}}.

Get IM get message fallback default value. -\/1, the default setting of the switch is to never ask the user to confirm the retransmission and never do the fallback 0 (default value), the default setting of the switch is to never ask the user to confirm the retransmission and always do the fallback. 1, the default setting of the switch is to always ask the user to confirm the retransmission as S\+MS.

set message fallback default value. -\/1, the default setting of the switch is to never ask the user to confirm the retransmission and never do the fallback 0 (default value), the default setting of the switch is to never ask the user to confirm the retransmission and always do the fallback. 1, the default setting of the switch is to always ask the user to confirm the retransmission as S\+MS
